I've uploaded a python code repository in the directory /testbed. Consider the following PR description:

<pr_description>
Inconsistent `Remove_Keys` behavior when running Loki output with multiple workers / threads
## Bug Report

**Describe the bug**

Apparently there's some sort of race condition in Loki output, where the keys in `Remove_Keys` are not always removed (sometimes they are partially removed, at random) when running the Loki output with multiple threads.

The bug does not seem to happen when omitting the `Workers` directive.

**To Reproduce:**
```ini
# fluentbit.conf
[INPUT]
    Name          dummy
    Interval_nsec 100
    Samples       100000
    Threaded      on
    Dummy         {"log": "message", "kubernetes": {"pod_name": "pod-name-01"}, "severity": "warn", "k8s_cluster_name": "cls01"}

[OUTPUT]
    Name                loki
    Match               *
    Remove_Keys         nonexistent, kubernetes, severity, k8s_cluster_name
    Structured_Metadata pod=$kubernetes['pod_name'], level=$severity
    Labels              cluster=$k8s_cluster_name
    Retry_Limit         0
    Workers             2
```

The Loki configuration file is the same one provided [here](https://raw.githubusercontent.com/grafana/loki/v3.4.1/cmd/loki/loki-local-config.yaml). Then:

```sh
# Terminal 1:
loki -config.file=loki.yaml -log.level=info

# Terminal 2:
fluent-bit -c fluentbit.conf
```

Leave fluent-bit running for a couple of seconds, then check the logs in a separate terminal:

```sh
logcli query '{cluster="cls01"}' --since=1m --limit=0
```

You will see that some of the keys weren't deleted; sometimes no keys are removed; sometimes a few random keys are removed, but not others.

Example:

```
...
2025-07-08T15:39:00-03:00 {} {"log":"message","k8s_cluster_name":"cls01"}
2025-07-08T15:39:00-03:00 {} {"log":"message"}
2025-07-08T15:39:00-03:00 {} {"log":"message"}
2025-07-08T15:39:00-03:00 {} {"log":"message"}
2025-07-08T15:39:00-03:00 {} {"log":"message"}
2025-07-08T15:39:00-03:00 {} {"log":"message"}
2025-07-08T15:39:00-03:00 {} {"log":"message"}
2025-07-08T15:39:00-03:00 {} {"log":"message"}
2025-07-08T15:39:00-03:00 {} {"log":"message"}
2025-07-08T15:39:00-03:00 {} {"log":"message","kubernetes":{"pod_name":"pod-name-01"},"severity":"warn","k8s_cluster_name":"cls01"}
2025-07-08T15:39:00-03:00 {} {"log":"message"}
2025-07-08T15:39:00-03:00 {} {"log":"message"}
2025-07-08T15:39:00-03:00 {} {"log":"message"}
2025-07-08T15:39:00-03:00 {} {"log":"message"}
2025-07-08T15:39:00-03:00 {} {"log":"message"}
2025-07-08T15:39:00-03:00 {} {"log":"message"}
2025-07-08T15:39:00-03:00 {} {"log":"message"}
2025-07-08T15:39:00-03:00 {} {"log":"message"}
2025-07-08T15:39:00-03:00 {} {"log":"message"}
2025-07-08T15:39:00-03:00 {} {"log":"message","kubernetes":{"pod_name":"pod-name-01"},"k8s_cluster_name":"cls01"}
```

I cannot reproduce the issue after removing the `Workers` directive.

**Expected behavior**
I'd expect the `Remove_Keys` setting to work consistently, always removing all keys, regardless of having enabled multiple workers or not.

**Your Environment**
<!--- Include as many relevant details about the environment you experienced the bug in -->
* Version used: 4.0.3; also 3.2.x that I run in my production GKE clusters
* Configuration: See above
* Environment name and version (e.g. Kubernetes? What version?): GKE; local
* Operating System and version: Linux 6.15.4-200.fc42.x86_64, but I also see the same issue in my GKE clusters
* Filters and plugins: See above

**Additional context**
The workaround for now is not using multiple workers for the Loki output.

</pr_description>

    38	struct flb_loki_dynamic_tenant_id_entry {
    39	    flb_sds_t value;
    40	    struct cfl_list _head;
    41	};
    42

    45	FLB_TLS_DEFINE(struct flb_loki_dynamic_tenant_id_entry,
    46	               thread_local_tenant_id);
    47	
    48	void initialize_thread_local_storage()

    53	static struct flb_loki_dynamic_tenant_id_entry *dynamic_tenant_id_create() {
    54	    struct flb_loki_dynamic_tenant_id_entry *entry;
    55	
    56	    entry = (struct flb_loki_dynamic_tenant_id_entry *) \
    57	        flb_calloc(1, sizeof(struct flb_loki_dynamic_tenant_id_entry));
    58	
    59	    if (entry != NULL) {
    60	        entry->value = NULL;
    61	
    62	        cfl_list_entry_init(&entry->_head);
    63	    }
    64	
    65	    return entry;
    66	}
    67	
    68	static void dynamic_tenant_id_destroy(struct flb_loki_dynamic_tenant_id_entry *entry) {
    69	    if (entry != NULL) {
    70	        if (entry->value != NULL) {
    71	            flb_sds_destroy(entry->value);
    72	
    73	            entry->value = NULL;
    74	        }
    75	
    76	        if (!cfl_list_entry_is_orphan(&entry->_head)) {
    77	            cfl_list_del(&entry->_head);
    78	        }
    79	
    80	        flb_free(entry);
    81	    }
    82	}

    85	{

    89	static inline void safe_sds_cat(flb_sds_t *buf, const char *str, int len)
    90	{
    91	    flb_sds_t tmp;
    92	
    93	    tmp = flb_sds_cat(*buf, str, len);
    94	    if (tmp) {
    95	        *buf = tmp;
    96	    }
    97	}
    98	
    99	static inline void normalize_cat(struct flb_ra_parser *rp, flb_sds_t *name)
   100	{
   101	    int sub;
   102	    int len;
   103	    char tmp[64];
   104	    struct mk_list *s_head;
   105	    struct flb_ra_key *key;
   106	    struct flb_ra_subentry *entry;
   107	
   108	    /* Iterate record accessor keys */
   109	    key = rp->key;
   110	    if (rp->type == FLB_RA_PARSER_STRING) {
   111	        safe_sds_cat(name, key->name, flb_sds_len(key->name));
   112	    }
   113	    else if (rp->type == FLB_RA_PARSER_KEYMAP) {
   114	        safe_sds_cat(name, key->name, flb_sds_len(key->name));
   115	        if (mk_list_size(key->subkeys) > 0) {
   116	            safe_sds_cat(name, "_", 1);
   117	        }
   118	
   119	        sub = 0;
   120	        mk_list_foreach(s_head, key->subkeys) {
   121	            entry = mk_list_entry(s_head, struct flb_ra_subentry, _head);
   122	
   123	            if (sub > 0) {
   124	                safe_sds_cat(name, "_", 1);
   125	            }
   126	            if (entry->type == FLB_RA_PARSER_STRING) {
   127	                safe_sds_cat(name, entry->str, flb_sds_len(entry->str));
   128	            }
   129	            else if (entry->type == FLB_RA_PARSER_ARRAY_ID) {
   130	                len = snprintf(tmp, sizeof(tmp) -1, "%d",
   131	                               entry->array_id);
   132	                safe_sds_cat(name, tmp, len);
   133	            }
   134	            sub++;
   135	        }
   136	    }
   137	}
   138	
   139	static flb_sds_t normalize_ra_key_name(struct flb_loki *ctx,
   140	                                       struct flb_record_accessor *ra)
   141	{
   142	    int c = 0;
   143	    flb_sds_t name;
   144	    struct mk_list *head;
   145	    struct flb_ra_parser *rp;
   146	
   147	    name = flb_sds_create_size(128);
   148	    if (!name) {
   149	        return NULL;
   150	    }
   151	
   152	    mk_list_foreach(head, &ra->list) {
   153	        rp = mk_list_entry(head, struct flb_ra_parser, _head);
   154	        if (c > 0) {
   155	            flb_sds_cat_safe(&name, "_", 1);
   156	        }
   157	        normalize_cat(rp, &name);
   158	        c++;
   159	    }
   160	
   161	    return name;
   162	}
   163	
   164	void flb_loki_kv_destroy(struct flb_loki_kv *kv)
   165	{
   166	    /* destroy key and value */
   167	    flb_sds_destroy(kv->key);
   168	    if (kv->val_type == FLB_LOKI_KV_STR) {
   169	        flb_sds_destroy(kv->str_val);
   170	    }
   171	    else if (kv->val_type == FLB_LOKI_KV_RA) {
   172	        flb_ra_destroy(kv->ra_val);
   173	    }
   174	
   175	    if (kv->ra_key) {
   176	        flb_ra_destroy(kv->ra_key);
   177	    }
   178	
   179	    if (kv->key_normalized) {
   180	        flb_sds_destroy(kv->key_normalized);
   181	    }
   182	
   183	    flb_free(kv);
   184	}
   185	
   186	int flb_loki_kv_append(struct flb_loki *ctx, struct mk_list *list, char *key, char *val)
   187	{
   188	    int ra_count = 0;
   189	    int k_len;
   190	    int ret;
   191	    struct flb_loki_kv *kv;
   192	
   193	    if (!key) {
   194	        return -1;
   195	    }
   196	
   197	    if (!val && key[0] != '$') {
   198	        return -1;
   199	    }
   200	
   201	    kv = flb_calloc(1, sizeof(struct flb_loki_kv));
   202	    if (!kv) {
   203	        flb_errno();
   204	        return -1;
   205	    }
   206	
   207	    k_len = strlen(key);
   208	    if (key[0] == '$' && k_len >= 2 && isdigit(key[1])) {
   209	        flb_plg_error(ctx->ins,
   210	                      "key name for record accessor cannot start with a number: %s",
   211	                      key);
   212	        flb_free(kv);
   213	        return -1;
   214	    }
   215	
   216	    kv->key = flb_sds_create(key);
   217	    if (!kv->key) {
   218	        flb_free(kv);
   219	        return -1;
   220	    }
   221	
   222	    /*
   223	     * If the key starts with a '$', it means its a record accessor pattern and
   224	     * the key value pair will be formed using the key name and it proper value.
   225	     */
   226	    if (key[0] == '$' && val == NULL) {
   227	        kv->ra_key = flb_ra_create(key, FLB_TRUE);
   228	        if (!kv->ra_key) {
   229	            flb_plg_error(ctx->ins,
   230	                          "invalid key record accessor pattern for key '%s'",
   231	                          key);
   232	            flb_loki_kv_destroy(kv);
   233	            return -1;
   234	        }
   235	
   236	        /* Normalize 'key name' using record accessor pattern */
   237	        kv->key_normalized = normalize_ra_key_name(ctx, kv->ra_key);
   238	        if (!kv->key_normalized) {
   239	            flb_plg_error(ctx->ins,
   240	                          "could not normalize key pattern name '%s'\n",
   241	                          kv->ra_key->pattern);
   242	            flb_loki_kv_destroy(kv);
   243	            return -1;
   244	        }
   245	        /* remove record keys placed as stream labels via 'labels' and 'label_keys' */
   246	        ret = flb_slist_add(&ctx->remove_keys_derived, key);
   247	        if (ret < 0) {
   248	            flb_loki_kv_destroy(kv);
   249	            return -1;
   250	        }
   251	        ra_count++;
   252	    }
   253	    else if (val[0] == '$') {
   254	        /* create a record accessor context */
   255	        kv->val_type = FLB_LOKI_KV_RA;
   256	        kv->ra_val = flb_ra_create(val, FLB_TRUE);
   257	        if (!kv->ra_val) {
   258	            flb_plg_error(ctx->ins,
   259	                          "invalid record accessor pattern for key '%s': %s",
   260	                          key, val);
   261	            flb_loki_kv_destroy(kv);
   262	            return -1;
   263	        }
   264	        ret = flb_slist_add(&ctx->remove_keys_derived, val);
   265	        if (ret < 0) {
   266	            flb_loki_kv_destroy(kv);
   267	            return -1;
   268	        }
   269	        ra_count++;
   270	    }
   271	    else {
   272	        kv->val_type = FLB_LOKI_KV_STR;
   273	        kv->str_val = flb_sds_create(val);
   274	        if (!kv->str_val) {
   275	            flb_loki_kv_destroy(kv);
   276	            return -1;
   277	        }
   278	    }
   279	    mk_list_add(&kv->_head, list);
   280	
   281	    /* return the number of record accessor values */
   282	    return ra_count;
   283	}
   284	
   285	static void flb_loki_kv_exit(struct flb_loki *ctx)
   286	{
   287	    struct mk_list *tmp;
   288	    struct mk_list *head;
   289	    struct flb_loki_kv *kv;
   290	
   291	    mk_list_foreach_safe(head, tmp, &ctx->labels_list) {
   292	        kv = mk_list_entry(head, struct flb_loki_kv, _head);
   293	
   294	        /* unlink and destroy */
   295	        mk_list_del(&kv->_head);
   296	        flb_loki_kv_destroy(kv);
   297	    }
   298	    mk_list_foreach_safe(head, tmp, &ctx->structured_metadata_list) {
   299	        kv = mk_list_entry(head, struct flb_loki_kv, _head);
   300	
   301	        /* unlink and destroy */
   302	        mk_list_del(&kv->_head);
   303	        flb_loki_kv_destroy(kv);
   304	    }
   305	    mk_list_foreach_safe(head, tmp, &ctx->structured_metadata_map_keys_list) {
   306	        kv = mk_list_entry(head, struct flb_loki_kv, _head);
   307	
   308	        /* unlink and destroy */
   309	        mk_list_del(&kv->_head);
   310	        flb_loki_kv_destroy(kv);
   311	    }
   312	}
   313	
   314	/* Pack a label key, it also perform sanitization of the characters */
   315	static int pack_label_key(msgpack_packer *mp_pck, char *key, int key_len)
   316	{
   317	    int i;
   318	    int k_len = key_len;
   319	    int is_digit = FLB_FALSE;
   320	    char *p;
   321	    size_t prev_size;
   322	
   323	    /* Normalize key name using the packed value */
   324	    if (isdigit(*key)) {
   325	        is_digit = FLB_TRUE;
   326	        k_len++;
   327	    }
   328	
   329	    /* key: pack the length */
   330	    msgpack_pack_str(mp_pck, k_len);
   331	    if (is_digit) {
   332	        msgpack_pack_str_body(mp_pck, "_", 1);
   333	    }
   334	
   335	    /* save the current offset */
   336	    prev_size = ((msgpack_sbuffer *) mp_pck->data)->size;
   337	
   338	    /* Pack the key name */
   339	    msgpack_pack_str_body(mp_pck, key, key_len);
   340	
   341	    /* 'p' will point to where the key was written */
   342	    p = (char *) (((msgpack_sbuffer*) mp_pck->data)->data + prev_size);
   343	
   344	    /* and sanitize the key characters */
   345	    for (i = 0; i < key_len; i++) {
   346	        if (!isalnum(p[i]) && p[i] != '_') {
   347	            p[i] = '_';
   348	        }
   349	    }
   350	
   351	    return 0;
   352	}
   353	
   354	static void pack_kv(struct flb_loki *ctx,
   355	                    msgpack_packer *mp_pck,
   356	                    char *tag, int tag_len,
   357	                    msgpack_object *map,
   358	                    struct flb_mp_map_header *mh,
   359	                    struct mk_list *list)
   360	{
   361	    struct mk_list *head;
   362	    struct flb_loki_kv *kv;
   363	    flb_sds_t ra_val;
   364	    mk_list_foreach(head, list) {
   365	        kv = mk_list_entry(head, struct flb_loki_kv, _head);
   366	
   367	        /* record accessor key/value pair */
   368	        if (kv->ra_key != NULL && kv->ra_val == NULL) {
   369	            ra_val = flb_ra_translate(kv->ra_key, tag, tag_len, *(map), NULL);
   370	            if (!ra_val || flb_sds_len(ra_val) == 0) {
   371	                /* if no value is retruned or if it's empty, just skip it */
   372	                flb_plg_debug(ctx->ins,
   373	                             "empty record accessor key translation for pattern: %s",
   374	                             kv->ra_key->pattern);
   375	            }
   376	            else {
   377	                /* Pack the key and value */
   378	                flb_mp_map_header_append(mh);
   379	
   380	                /* We skip the first '$' character since it won't be valid in Loki */
   381	                pack_label_key(mp_pck, kv->key_normalized,
   382	                               flb_sds_len(kv->key_normalized));
   383	
   384	                msgpack_pack_str(mp_pck, flb_sds_len(ra_val));
   385	                msgpack_pack_str_body(mp_pck, ra_val, flb_sds_len(ra_val));
   386	            }
   387	
   388	            if (ra_val) {
   389	                flb_sds_destroy(ra_val);
   390	            }
   391	            continue;
   392	        }
   393	
   394	        /*
   395	         * The code is a bit duplicated to be able to manage the exception of an
   396	         * invalid or empty value, on that case the k/v is skipped.
   397	         */
   398	        if (kv->val_type == FLB_LOKI_KV_STR) {
   399	            flb_mp_map_header_append(mh);
   400	            msgpack_pack_str(mp_pck, flb_sds_len(kv->key));
   401	            msgpack_pack_str_body(mp_pck, kv->key, flb_sds_len(kv->key));
   402	            msgpack_pack_str(mp_pck, flb_sds_len(kv->str_val));
   403	            msgpack_pack_str_body(mp_pck, kv->str_val, flb_sds_len(kv->str_val));
   404	        }
   405	        else if (kv->val_type == FLB_LOKI_KV_RA) {
   406	            /* record accessor type */
   407	            ra_val = flb_ra_translate(kv->ra_val, tag, tag_len, *(map), NULL);
   408	            if (!ra_val || flb_sds_len(ra_val) == 0) {
   409	                flb_plg_debug(ctx->ins, "could not translate record accessor");
   410	            }
   411	            else {
   412	                flb_mp_map_header_append(mh);
   413	                msgpack_pack_str(mp_pck, flb_sds_len(kv->key));
   414	                msgpack_pack_str_body(mp_pck, kv->key, flb_sds_len(kv->key));
   415	                msgpack_pack_str(mp_pck, flb_sds_len(ra_val));
   416	                msgpack_pack_str_body(mp_pck, ra_val, flb_sds_len(ra_val));
   417	            }
   418	
   419	            if (ra_val) {
   420	                flb_sds_destroy(ra_val);
   421	            }
   422	        }
   423	    }
   424	}
   425	
   426	/*
   427	 * Similar to pack_kv above, except will only use msgpack_objects of type
   428	 * MSGPACK_OBJECT_MAP, and will iterate over the keys adding each entry as a
   429	 * separate item. Non-string map values are serialised to JSON, as Loki requires
   430	 * all values to be strings.
   431	*/
   432	static void pack_maps(struct flb_loki *ctx,
   433	                        msgpack_packer *mp_pck,
   434	                        char *tag, int tag_len,
   435	                        msgpack_object *map,
   436	                        struct flb_mp_map_header *mh,
   437	                        struct mk_list *list)
   438	{
   439	    struct mk_list *head;
   440	    struct flb_loki_kv *kv;
   441	
   442	    msgpack_object *start_key;
   443	    msgpack_object *out_key;
   444	    msgpack_object *out_val;
   445	
   446	    msgpack_object_map accessed_map;
   447	    uint32_t accessed_map_index;
   448	    msgpack_object_kv accessed_map_kv;
   449	
   450	    char *accessed_map_val_json;
   451	
   452	    mk_list_foreach(head, list) {
   453	        /* get the flb_loki_kv for this iteration of the loop */
   454	        kv = mk_list_entry(head, struct flb_loki_kv, _head);
   455	
   456	        /* record accessor key/value pair */
   457	        if (kv->ra_key != NULL && kv->ra_val == NULL) {
   458	
   459	            /* try to get the value for the record accessor */
   460	            if (flb_ra_get_kv_pair(kv->ra_key, *map, &start_key, &out_key, &out_val)
   461	                == 0) {
   462	
   463	                /*
   464	                 * we require the value to be a map, or it doesn't make sense as
   465	                 * this is adding a map's key / values
   466	                 */
   467	                if (out_val->type != MSGPACK_OBJECT_MAP || out_val->via.map.size <= 0) {
   468	                    flb_plg_debug(ctx->ins, "No valid map data found for key %s",
   469	                                  kv->ra_key->pattern);
   470	                }
   471	                else {
   472	                    accessed_map = out_val->via.map;
   473	
   474	                    /* for each entry in the accessed map... */
   475	                    for (accessed_map_index = 0; accessed_map_index < accessed_map.size;
   476	                         accessed_map_index++) {
   477	
   478	                        /* get the entry */
   479	                        accessed_map_kv = accessed_map.ptr[accessed_map_index];
   480	
   481	                        /* Pack the key and value */
   482	                        flb_mp_map_header_append(mh);
   483	
   484	                        pack_label_key(mp_pck, (char*) accessed_map_kv.key.via.str.ptr,
   485	                                       accessed_map_kv.key.via.str.size);
   486	
   487	                        /* If the value is a string, just pack it... */
   488	                        if (accessed_map_kv.val.type == MSGPACK_OBJECT_STR) {
   489	                            msgpack_pack_str_with_body(mp_pck,
   490	                                                       accessed_map_kv.val.via.str.ptr,
   491	                                                       accessed_map_kv.val.via.str.size);
   492	                        }
   493	                        /*
   494	                         * ...otherwise convert value to JSON string, as Loki always
   495	                         * requires a string value
   496	                         */
   497	                        else {
   498	                            accessed_map_val_json = flb_msgpack_to_json_str(1024,
   499	                                &accessed_map_kv.val);
   500	                            if (accessed_map_val_json) {
   501	                                msgpack_pack_str_with_body(mp_pck, accessed_map_val_json,
   502	                                                         strlen(accessed_map_val_json));
   503	                                flb_free(accessed_map_val_json);
   504	                            }
   505	                        }
   506	                    }
   507	                }
   508	            }
   509	        }
   510	    }
   511	}

   994	static int prepare_remove_keys(struct flb_loki *ctx)
   995	{
   996	    int ret;
   997	    int len;
   998	    int size;
   999	    char *tmp;
  1000	    struct mk_list *head;
  1001	    struct flb_slist_entry *entry;

  1005

  1008	        mk_list_foreach(head, ctx->remove_keys) {
  1009	            entry = mk_list_entry(head, struct flb_slist_entry, _head);
  1010	
  1011	            if (entry->str[0] != '$') {
  1012	                tmp = flb_malloc(flb_sds_len(entry->str) + 2);
  1013	                if (!tmp) {
  1014	                    flb_errno();
  1015	                    continue;
  1016	                }

  1019	                    len = flb_sds_len(entry->str);

  1021	                    tmp[len + 1] = '\0';
  1022	                    len++;
  1023	                }
  1024	            }
  1025	            else {
  1026	                tmp = entry->str;
  1027	                len = flb_sds_len(entry->str);
  1028	            }
  1029	
  1030	            ret = key_is_duplicated(patterns, tmp, len);
  1031	            if (ret == FLB_TRUE) {
  1032	                if (entry->str != tmp) {
  1033	                    flb_free(tmp);
  1034	                }
  1035	                continue;
  1036	            }
  1037	
  1038	            ret = flb_slist_add_n(patterns, tmp, len);
  1039	            if (entry->str != tmp) {
  1040	                flb_free(tmp);
  1041	            }
  1042	            if (ret < 0) {
  1043	                return -1;
  1044	            }
  1045	        }

  1048	        if (size > 0) {
  1049	            ctx->remove_mpa = flb_mp_accessor_create(patterns);

    38	/* don't do this at home */
    39	#define pack_uint16(buf, d) _msgpack_store16(buf, (uint16_t) d)
    40	#define pack_uint32(buf, d) _msgpack_store32(buf, (uint32_t) d)
    41	
    42	/* Return the number of msgpack serialized events in the buffer */
    43	int flb_mp_count(const void *data, size_t bytes)
    44	{
    45	    return flb_mp_count_remaining(data, bytes, NULL);
    46	}
    47	
    48	int flb_mp_count_remaining(const void *data, size_t bytes, size_t *remaining_bytes)
    49	{
    50	    size_t remaining;
    51	    int count = 0;
    52	    mpack_reader_t reader;
    53	
    54	    mpack_reader_init_data(&reader, (const char *) data, bytes);
    55	    for (;;) {
    56	        remaining = mpack_reader_remaining(&reader, NULL);
    57	        if (!remaining) {
    58	            break;
    59	        }
    60	        mpack_discard(&reader);
    61	        if (mpack_reader_error(&reader)) {
    62	            break;
    63	        }
    64	        count++;
    65	    }
    66	
    67	    if (remaining_bytes) {
    68	        *remaining_bytes = remaining;
    69	    }
    70	    mpack_reader_destroy(&reader);
    71	    return count;
    72	}
    73	
    74	int flb_mp_validate_metric_chunk(const void *data, size_t bytes,
    75	                                 int *out_series, size_t *processed_bytes)
    76	{
    77	    int ret;
    78	    int ok = CMT_DECODE_MSGPACK_SUCCESS;
    79	    int count = 0;
    80	    size_t off = 0;
    81	    size_t pre_off = 0;
    82	    struct cmt *cmt;
    83	
    84	    while ((ret = cmt_decode_msgpack_create(&cmt,
    85	                                            (char *) data, bytes, &off)) == ok) {
    86	        cmt_destroy(cmt);
    87	        count++;
    88	        pre_off = off;
    89	    }
    90	
    91	    switch (ret) {
    92	        case CMT_DECODE_MSGPACK_INVALID_ARGUMENT_ERROR:
    93	        case CMT_DECODE_MSGPACK_CORRUPT_INPUT_DATA_ERROR:
    94	        case CMT_DECODE_MSGPACK_CONSUME_ERROR:
    95	        case CMT_DECODE_MSGPACK_ENGINE_ERROR:
    96	        case CMT_DECODE_MSGPACK_PENDING_MAP_ENTRIES:
    97	        case CMT_DECODE_MSGPACK_PENDING_ARRAY_ENTRIES:
    98	        case CMT_DECODE_MSGPACK_UNEXPECTED_KEY_ERROR:
    99	        case CMT_DECODE_MSGPACK_UNEXPECTED_DATA_TYPE_ERROR:
   100	        case CMT_DECODE_MSGPACK_DICTIONARY_LOOKUP_ERROR:
   101	        case CMT_DECODE_MSGPACK_VERSION_ERROR:
   102	            goto error;
   103	    }
   104	
   105	    if (ret == CMT_DECODE_MSGPACK_INSUFFICIENT_DATA && off == bytes) {
   106	        *out_series = count;
   107	        *processed_bytes = pre_off;
   108	        return 0;
   109	    }
   110	
   111	error:
   112	    *out_series = count;
   113	    *processed_bytes = pre_off;
   114	
   115	    return -1;
   116	}
   117	
   118	int flb_mp_validate_log_chunk(const void *data, size_t bytes,
   119	                              int *out_records, size_t *processed_bytes)
   120	{
   121	    int ret;
   122	    int count = 0;
   123	    size_t off = 0;
   124	    size_t pre_off = 0;
   125	    size_t ptr_size;
   126	    unsigned char *ptr;
   127	    msgpack_object array;
   128	    msgpack_object ts;
   129	    msgpack_object header;
   130	    msgpack_object record;
   131	    msgpack_object metadata;
   132	    msgpack_unpacked result;
   133	
   134	    msgpack_unpacked_init(&result);
   135	    while (msgpack_unpack_next(&result, data, bytes, &off) == MSGPACK_UNPACK_SUCCESS) {
   136	        array = result.data;
   137	
   138	        if (array.type != MSGPACK_OBJECT_ARRAY) {
   139	            /*
   140	             * Sometimes there is a special case: Chunks might have extra zero
   141	             * bytes at the end of a record, meaning: no more records. This is not
   142	             * an error and actually it happens if a previous run of Fluent Bit
   143	             * was stopped/killed before to adjust the file size.
   144	             *
   145	             * Just validate if all bytes are zero, if so, adjust counters
   146	             * and return zero.
   147	             */
   148	            ptr = (unsigned char *) (data);
   149	            ptr += pre_off;
   150	            if (ptr[0] != 0) {
   151	                goto error;
   152	            }
   153	
   154	            ptr_size = bytes - pre_off;
   155	            ret = memcmp(ptr, ptr + 1, ptr_size - 1);
   156	            if (ret == 0) {
   157	                /*
   158	                 * The chunk is valid, just let the caller know the last processed
   159	                 * valid byte.
   160	                 */
   161	                msgpack_unpacked_destroy(&result);
   162	                *out_records = count;
   163	                *processed_bytes = pre_off;
   164	                return 0;
   165	            }
   166	            goto error;
   167	        }
   168	
   169	        if (array.via.array.size != 2) {
   170	            goto error;
   171	        }
   172	
   173	        header = array.via.array.ptr[0];
   174	        record = array.via.array.ptr[1];
   175	
   176	        if (header.type == MSGPACK_OBJECT_ARRAY) {
   177	            if (header.via.array.size != 2) {
   178	                goto error;
   179	            }
   180	
   181	            ts = header.via.array.ptr[0];
   182	            metadata = header.via.array.ptr[1];
   183	
   184	            if (metadata.type != MSGPACK_OBJECT_MAP) {
   185	                goto error;
   186	            }
   187	        }
   188	        else {
   189	            ts = header;
   190	        }
   191	
   192	        if (ts.type != MSGPACK_OBJECT_POSITIVE_INTEGER &&
   193	            ts.type != MSGPACK_OBJECT_FLOAT &&
   194	            ts.type != MSGPACK_OBJECT_EXT) {
   195	            goto error;
   196	        }
   197	
   198	        if (record.type != MSGPACK_OBJECT_MAP) {
   199	            goto error;
   200	        }

   537	static inline int accessor_sub_pack(struct flb_mp_accessor *mpa,
   538	                                    int* matched_indexes,
   539	                                    int match_count,
   540	                                    msgpack_packer *mp_pck,
   541	                                    msgpack_object *key,
   542	                                    msgpack_object *val)
   543	{
   544	    int i;
   545	    int ret;
   546	    msgpack_object *k;
   547	    msgpack_object *v;
   548	    struct flb_mp_map_header mh;
   549	    struct flb_mp_accessor_match *match;
   550	
   551	    for (i = 0; i < match_count; i++) {
   552	        match = &mpa->matches[matched_indexes[i]];
   553	        if (match->key == key || match->key == val) {
   554	            return FLB_FALSE;
   555	        }
   556	    }
   557	
   558	    if (key) {
   559	        msgpack_pack_object(mp_pck, *key);
   560	    }
   561	
   562	    if (val->type == MSGPACK_OBJECT_MAP) {
   563	        flb_mp_map_header_init(&mh, mp_pck);
   564	        for (i = 0; i < val->via.map.size; i++) {
   565	            k = &val->via.map.ptr[i].key;
   566	            v = &val->via.map.ptr[i].val;
   567	
   568	            ret = accessor_sub_pack(mpa, matched_indexes, match_count, mp_pck, k, v);
   569	            if (ret == FLB_TRUE) {
   570	                flb_mp_map_header_append(&mh);
   571	            }
   572	        }
   573	        flb_mp_map_header_end(&mh);
   574	    }
   575	    else if (val->type == MSGPACK_OBJECT_ARRAY) {
   576	        flb_mp_array_header_init(&mh, mp_pck);
   577	        for (i = 0; i < val->via.array.size; i++) {
   578	            v = &val->via.array.ptr[i];
   579	            ret = accessor_sub_pack(mpa, matched_indexes, match_count, mp_pck, NULL, v);
   580	            if (ret == FLB_TRUE) {
   581	                flb_mp_array_header_append(&mh);
   582	            }
   583	        }
   584	        flb_mp_array_header_end(&mh);
   585	    }
   586	    else {
   587	        msgpack_pack_object(mp_pck, *val);
   588	    }
   589	
   590	    return FLB_TRUE;
   591	}

   650	    if (matches == 0) {
   651	        return FLB_FALSE;
   652	    }
   653	
   654	    /* Some rules matched, compose a new outgoing buffer */
   655	    msgpack_sbuffer_init(&mp_sbuf);
   656	    msgpack_packer_init(&mp_pck, &mp_sbuf, msgpack_sbuffer_write);
   657	
   658	    /* Initialize map */
   659	    flb_mp_map_header_init(&mh, &mp_pck);
   660	
   661	    /* Initialize array of matching indexes to properly handle sibling keys */
   662	    matched_indexes = flb_malloc(sizeof(int) * matches);
   663	    if (!matched_indexes) {
   664	        flb_errno();
   665	        return -1;
   666	    }
   667	
   668	    for (i = 0; i < map->via.map.size; i++) {
   669	        key = &map->via.map.ptr[i].key;
   670	        val = &map->via.map.ptr[i].val;
   671	
   672	        /*
   673	         * For every entry on the path, check if we should do a step-by-step
   674	         * repackaging or just pack the whole object.
   675	         *
   676	         * Find all matching rules that match this 'key'. Return the number of matches or 0
   677	         * if no matches were found. Found matches are stored in the 'matched_indexes' array.
   678	         */
   679	        ret = accessor_key_find_matches(mpa, key, matched_indexes);
   680	        if (ret == 0) {
   681	            /* No matches, it's ok to pack the kv pair */
   682	            flb_mp_map_header_append(&mh);
   683	            msgpack_pack_object(&mp_pck, *key);
   684	            msgpack_pack_object(&mp_pck, *val);
   685	        }
   686	        else {
   687	            /* The key has a match. Now we do a step-by-step packaging */

   468	    mpa = flb_calloc(1, sizeof(struct flb_mp_accessor));
   469	    if (!mpa) {
   470	        flb_errno();
   471	        return NULL;
   472	    }
   473	    mk_list_init(&mpa->ra_list);
   474

   491	    }

str_replace_editor insert /testbed/src/flb_mp.c    --new_str 'struct flb_mp_accessor_match* flb_mp_accessor_get_matches(struct flb_mp_accessor *mpa,
                                                          msgpack_object *map,
                                                          int *out_matches)
{
    int rule_id = 0;
    int matches = 0;
    int ret;
    msgpack_object *s_key;
    msgpack_object *o_key;
    msgpack_object *o_val;
    struct mk_list *head;
    struct flb_mp_accessor_match *match;
    struct flb_mp_accessor_ra *mp_ra;
    struct flb_mp_accessor_match *matches_results;

    /* Reset matches cache */
    memset(mpa->matches, '"'"'\0'"'"', mpa->matches_size);

    mk_list_foreach(head, &mpa->ra_list) {
        mp_ra = mk_list_entry(head, struct flb_mp_accessor_ra, _head);

        if (mp_ra->is_active == FLB_FALSE) {
            rule_id++;
            continue;
        }

        /* Apply the record accessor rule against the map */
        ret = flb_ra_get_kv_pair(mp_ra->ra, *map, &s_key, &o_key, &o_val);
        if (ret == 0) {
            /* There is a match, register in the matches table */
            match = &mpa->matches[rule_id];
            match->matched = FLB_TRUE;
            match->start_key = s_key;        /* Initial key path that matched */
            match->key = o_key;              /* Final key that matched */
            match->val = o_val;              /* Final value */
            match->ra = mp_ra->ra;           /* Record accessor context */
            matches++;
        }
        rule_id++;
    }

    if (matches == 0) {
        *out_matches = 0;
        return NULL;
    }

    matches_results = flb_calloc(matches, sizeof(struct flb_mp_accessor_match));
    if (!matches_results) {
        *out_matches = 0;
        return NULL;
    }

    matches = 0;
    for (rule_id = 0; rule_id < mk_list_size(&mpa->ra_list); rule_id++) {
        if (mpa->matches[rule_id].matched) {
            memcpy(&matches_results[matches], &mpa->matches[rule_id], sizeof(struct flb_mp_accessor_match));
            matches++;
        }
    }

    *out_matches = matches;
    return matches_results;
}

int flb_mp_accessor_keys_remove_by_matches(struct flb_mp_accessor *mpa,
                                           msgpack_object *map,
                                           struct flb_mp_accessor_match *matches_results,
                                           int matches,
                                           void **out_buf, size_t *out_size)
{
    int i;
    int ret;
    int* matched_indexes;
    msgpack_object *key;
    msgpack_object *val;
    struct flb_mp_map_header mh;
    msgpack_sbuffer mp_sbuf;
    msgpack_packer mp_pck;

    if (matches == 0) {
        return FLB_FALSE;
    }

   594	 * Remove keys or nested keys from a map. It compose the final result in a
   595	 * new buffer. On error, it returns -1, if the map was modified it returns FLB_TRUE,
   596	 * if no modification was required it returns FLB_FALSE.
   597	 */
   598	struct flb_mp_accessor_match* flb_mp_accessor_get_matches(struct flb_mp_accessor *mpa,
   599	                                                          msgpack_object *map,
   600	                                                          int *out_matches)
   601	{
   602	    int rule_id = 0;
   603	    int matches = 0;
   604	    int ret;
   605	    msgpack_object *s_key;
   606	    msgpack_object *o_key;
   607	    msgpack_object *o_val;
   608	    struct mk_list *head;
   609	    struct flb_mp_accessor_match *match;
   610	    struct flb_mp_accessor_ra *mp_ra;
   611	    struct flb_mp_accessor_match *matches_results;
   612	
   613	    /* Reset matches cache */
   614	    memset(mpa->matches, '\0', mpa->matches_size);
   615	
   616	    mk_list_foreach(head, &mpa->ra_list) {
   617	        mp_ra = mk_list_entry(head, struct flb_mp_accessor_ra, _head);
   618	
   619	        if (mp_ra->is_active == FLB_FALSE) {
   620	            rule_id++;
   621	            continue;
   622	        }
   623	
   624	        /* Apply the record accessor rule against the map */
   625	        ret = flb_ra_get_kv_pair(mp_ra->ra, *map, &s_key, &o_key, &o_val);
   626	        if (ret == 0) {
   627	            /* There is a match, register in the matches table */
   628	            match = &mpa->matches[rule_id];
   629	            match->matched = FLB_TRUE;
   630	            match->start_key = s_key;        /* Initial key path that matched */
   631	            match->key = o_key;              /* Final key that matched */
   632	            match->val = o_val;              /* Final value */
   633	            match->ra = mp_ra->ra;           /* Record accessor context */
   634	            matches++;
   635	        }
   636	        rule_id++;
   637	    }
   638	
   639	    if (matches == 0) {
   640	        *out_matches = 0;
   641	        return NULL;
   642	    }
   643	
   644	    matches_results = flb_calloc(matches, sizeof(struct flb_mp_accessor_match));
   645	    if (!matches_results) {
   646	        *out_matches = 0;
   647	        return NULL;
   648	    }
   649	
   650	    matches = 0;
   651	    for (rule_id = 0; rule_id < mk_list_size(&mpa->ra_list); rule_id++) {
   652	        if (mpa->matches[rule_id].matched) {
   653	            memcpy(&matches_results[matches], &mpa->matches[rule_id], sizeof(struct flb_mp_accessor_match));
   654	            matches++;
   655	        }
   656	    }
   657	
   658	    *out_matches = matches;
   659	    return matches_results;
   660	}

    42	/* Return the number of msgpack serialized events in the buffer */
    43	int flb_mp_count(const void *data, size_t bytes)
    44	{
    45	    return flb_mp_count_remaining(data, bytes, NULL);
    46	}
    47	
    48	int flb_mp_count_remaining(const void *data, size_t bytes, size_t *remaining_bytes)
    49	{
    50	    size_t remaining;
    51	    int count = 0;
    52	    mpack_reader_t reader;
    53	
    54	    mpack_reader_init_data(&reader, (const char *) data, bytes);
    55	    for (;;) {
    56	        remaining = mpack_reader_remaining(&reader, NULL);
    57	        if (!remaining) {
    58	            break;
    59	        }
    60	        mpack_discard(&reader);
    61	        if (mpack_reader_error(&reader)) {
    62	            break;
    63	        }
    64	        count++;
    65	    }
    66	
    67	    if (remaining_bytes) {
    68	        *remaining_bytes = remaining;
    69	    }
    70	    mpack_reader_destroy(&reader);
    71	    return count;
    72	}

   118	int flb_mp_validate_log_chunk(const void *data, size_t bytes,
   119	                              int *out_records, size_t *processed_bytes)
   120	{
   121	    int ret;
   122	    int count = 0;
   123	    size_t off = 0;
   124	    size_t pre_off = 0;
   125	    size_t ptr_size;
   126	    unsigned char *ptr;
   127	    msgpack_object array;
   128	    msgpack_object ts;
   129	    msgpack_object header;
   130	    msgpack_object record;
   131	    msgpack_object metadata;
   132	    msgpack_unpacked result;
   133	
   134	    msgpack_unpacked_init(&result);
   135	    while (msgpack_unpack_next(&result, data, bytes, &off) == MSGPACK_UNPACK_SUCCESS) {
   136	        array = result.data;
   137	
   138	        if (array.type != MSGPACK_OBJECT_ARRAY) {
   139	            /*
   140	             * Sometimes there is a special case: Chunks might have extra zero
   141	             * bytes at the end of a record, meaning: no more records. This is not
   142	             * an error and actually it happens if a previous run of Fluent Bit
   143	             * was stopped/killed before to adjust the file size.
   144	             *
   145	             * Just validate if all bytes are zero, if so, adjust counters
   146	             * and return zero.
   147	             */
   148	            ptr = (unsigned char *) (data);
   149	            ptr += pre_off;
   150	            if (ptr[0] != 0) {
   151	                goto error;
   152	            }
   153	
   154	            ptr_size = bytes - pre_off;
   155	            ret = memcmp(ptr, ptr + 1, ptr_size - 1);
   156	            if (ret == 0) {
   157	                /*
   158	                 * The chunk is valid, just let the caller know the last processed
   159	                 * valid byte.
   160	                 */
   161	                msgpack_unpacked_destroy(&result);
   162	                *out_records = count;
   163	                *processed_bytes = pre_off;
   164	                return 0;
   165	            }
   166	            goto error;
   167	        }
   168	
   169	        if (array.via.array.size != 2) {
   170	            goto error;
   171	        }
   172	
   173	        header = array.via.array.ptr[0];
   174	        record = array.via.array.ptr[1];
   175	
   176	        if (header.type == MSGPACK_OBJECT_ARRAY) {
   177	            if (header.via.array.size != 2) {
   178	                goto error;
   179	            }
   180	
   181	            ts = header.via.array.ptr[0];
   182	            metadata = header.via.array.ptr[1];
   183	
   184	            if (metadata.type != MSGPACK_OBJECT_MAP) {
   185	                goto error;
   186	            }
   187	        }
   188	        else {
   189	            ts = header;
   190	        }
   191	
   192	        if (ts.type != MSGPACK_OBJECT_POSITIVE_INTEGER &&
   193	            ts.type != MSGPACK_OBJECT_FLOAT &&
   194	            ts.type != MSGPACK_OBJECT_EXT) {
   195	            goto error;
   196	        }
   197	
   198	        if (record.type != MSGPACK_OBJECT_MAP) {
   199	            goto error;
   200	        }

str_replace_editor str_replace /testbed/src/flb_mp.c   --old_str 'struct flb_mp_accessor_match* flb_mp_accessor_get_matches(struct flb_mp_accessor *mpa,
                                                          msgpack_object *map,
                                                          int *out_matches)
{
    int rule_id = 0;
    int matches = 0;
    int ret;
    msgpack_object *s_key;
    msgpack_object *o_key;
    msgpack_object *o_val;
    struct mk_list *head;
    struct flb_mp_accessor_match *match;
    struct flb_mp_accessor_ra *mp_ra;
    struct flb_mp_accessor_match *matches_results;

    /* Reset matches cache */
    memset(mpa->matches, '"'"'\0'"'"', mpa->matches_size);

    mk_list_foreach(head, &mpa->ra_list) {
        mp_ra = mk_list_entry(head, struct flb_mp_accessor_ra, _head);

        if (mp_ra->is_active == FLB_FALSE) {
            rule_id++;
            continue;
        }

        /* Apply the record accessor rule against the map */
        ret = flb_ra_get_kv_pair(mp_ra->ra, *map, &s_key, &o_key, &o_val);
        if (ret == 0) {
            /* There is a match, register in the matches table */
            match = &mpa->matches[rule_id];
            match->matched = FLB_TRUE;
            match->start_key = s_key;        /* Initial key path that matched */
            match->key = o_key;              /* Final key that matched */
            match->val = o_val;              /* Final value */
            match->ra = mp_ra->ra;           /* Record accessor context */
            matches++;
        }
        rule_id++;
    }

    if (matches == 0) {
        *out_matches = 0;
        return NULL;
    }

    matches_results = flb_calloc(matches, sizeof(struct flb_mp_accessor_match));
    if (!matches_results) {
        *out_matches = 0;
        return NULL;
    }

    matches = 0;
    for (rule_id = 0; rule_id < mk_list_size(&mpa->ra_list); rule_id++) {
        if (mpa->matches[rule_id].matched) {
            memcpy(&matches_results[matches], &mpa->matches[rule_id], sizeof(struct flb_mp_accessor_match));
            matches++;
        }
    }

    *out_matches = matches;
    return matches_results;
}

    msgpack_packer mp_pck;

    if (matches == 0) {
        return FLB_FALSE;
    }

    /* Set the matches back into mpa for current processing */
    memset(mpa->matches, '"'"'\0'"'"', mpa->matches_size);
    for (i = 0; i < matches; i++) {
        /* We need to find the correct rule_id in mpa->ra_list if we wanted to be perfectly correct,

           Since matches_results was just a copy, this is slightly complex.

                                msgpack_object *map,
                                void **out_buf, size_t *out_size)

' --new_str '/*
 * Remove keys or nested keys from a map. It compose the final result in a
 * new buffer. On error, it returns -1, if the map was modified it returns FLB_TRUE,
 * if no modification was required it returns FLB_FALSE.
 */
int flb_mp_accessor_keys_remove(struct flb_mp_accessor *mpa,
                                msgpack_object *map,
                                void **out_buf, size_t *out_size)
{
    int i;
    int ret;
    int rule_id = 0;
    int matches = 0;
    int* matched_indexes;
    msgpack_object *key;
    msgpack_object *val;
    msgpack_object *s_key;
    msgpack_object *o_key;
    msgpack_object *o_val;
    struct mk_list *head;
    struct flb_mp_accessor_match *match;
    struct flb_mp_accessor_ra *mp_ra;
    struct flb_mp_map_header mh;
    msgpack_sbuffer mp_sbuf;
    msgpack_packer mp_pck;
    struct flb_mp_accessor_match *local_matches;
    size_t local_matches_size;

    if (map->via.map.size == 0) {
        return FLB_FALSE;
    }

    local_matches_size = mpa->matches_size;
    local_matches = flb_calloc(1, local_matches_size);
    if (!local_matches) {
        flb_errno();
        return -1;
    }

    mk_list_foreach(head, &mpa->ra_list) {
        mp_ra = mk_list_entry(head, struct flb_mp_accessor_ra, _head);

        if (mp_ra->is_active == FLB_FALSE) {
            rule_id++;
            continue;
        }

        /* Apply the record accessor rule against the map */
        ret = flb_ra_get_kv_pair(mp_ra->ra, *map, &s_key, &o_key, &o_val);
        if (ret == 0) {
            /* There is a match, register in the matches table */
            match = &local_matches[rule_id];
            match->matched = FLB_TRUE;
            match->start_key = s_key;        /* Initial key path that matched */
            match->key = o_key;              /* Final key that matched */
            match->val = o_val;              /* Final value */
            match->ra = mp_ra->ra;           /* Record accessor context */
            matches++;
        }
        rule_id++;
    }

    /* If no matches, no modifications were made */
    if (matches == 0) {
        flb_free(local_matches);
        return FLB_FALSE;
    }

    /* Some rules matched, compose a new outgoing buffer */
    msgpack_sbuffer_init(&mp_sbuf);
    msgpack_packer_init(&mp_pck, &mp_sbuf, msgpack_sbuffer_write);

    /* Initialize map */
    flb_mp_map_header_init(&mh, &mp_pck);

    /* Initialize array of matching indexes to properly handle sibling keys */
    matched_indexes = flb_malloc(sizeof(int) * matches);
    if (!matched_indexes) {
        flb_errno();
        flb_free(local_matches);
        msgpack_sbuffer_destroy(&mp_sbuf);
        return -1;
    }

    for (i = 0; i < map->via.map.size; i++) {
        key = &map->via.map.ptr[i].key;
        val = &map->via.map.ptr[i].val;

        /*
         * For every entry on the path, check if we should do a step-by-step
         * repackaging or just pack the whole object.
         *
         * Find all matching rules that match this '"'"'key'"'"'. Return the number of matches or 0
         * if no matches were found. Found matches are stored in the '"'"'matched_indexes'"'"' array.
         */
        
        int match_count = 0;
        int out_index = 0;
        int ra_count = mk_list_size(&mpa->ra_list);
        for (int j = 0; j < ra_count; j++) {
            match = &local_matches[j];
            if (match->matched == FLB_FALSE) {
                continue;
            }

            if (match->start_key == key) {
                match_count++;
                matched_indexes[out_index++] = j;
            }
        }

        if (match_count == 0) {
            /* No matches, it'"'"'s ok to pack the kv pair */
            flb_mp_map_header_append(&mh);
            msgpack_pack_object(&mp_pck, *key);
            msgpack_pack_object(&mp_pck, *val);
        }
        else {
            /* The key has a match. Now we do a step-by-step packaging */
            
            /* Since accessor_sub_pack still uses mpa->matches, we need to temporarily swap it 
               or rewrite accessor_sub_pack. Swapping is easier but needs a lock if multiple 
               threads use the same mpa. But the point is to make it thread safe.
            */
            /* Actually, accessor_sub_pack just needs the match information. Let'"'"'s rewrite it or 
               pass local_matches to it.
            */
            
            /* To keep it simple and correct, I will use a local copy of mpa->matches inside accessor_sub_pack as well. 
               This means accessor_sub_pack also needs to be updated.
            */
            
            /* I'"'"'ll stop here and rethink. The easiest way is to protect mpa->matches with a mutex inside flb_mp_accessor_keys_remove, 
               but wait, the caller might be using workers. If they all use the same mpa, they will contend. 
               The PR says Workers 2. Each worker has its own thread. 
            */
            /* If I use a lock, it will work but might be slow. But the current implementation is definitely not thread-safe. */
            
            /* Let'"'"'s see how mpa is created and stored. In Loki, it'"'"'s in ctx->remove_mpa. 
               ctx is the plugin instance. In Fluent Bit, plugin instances are shared among workers? 
               Yes, but some plugins have thread-local data. 
            */
            
            /* If I change accessor_sub_pack and accessor_key_find_matches to take the matches array as an argument, it becomes thread-safe. */
            
            flb_free(local_matches); /* dummy to satisfy the logic for now, I will redo the whole thing */
            flb_free(matched_indexes);
            msgpack_sbuffer_destroy(&mp_sbuf);
            return -1; 
        }
    }
    return -1;
}

/*
 * Remove keys or nested keys from a map. It compose the final result in a
 * new buffer. On error, it returns -1, if the map was modified it returns FLB_TRUE,
 * if no modification was required it returns FLB_FALSE.
 */
/*
 * Remove keys or nested keys from a map. It compose the final result in a
 * new buffer. On error, it returns -1, if the map was modified it returns FLB_TRUE,
 * if no modification was required it returns FLB_FALSE.
 */
int flb_mp_accessor_keys_remove(struct flb_mp_accessor *mpa,
                                msgpack_object *map,
                                void **out_buf, size_t *out_size)
{
    int i;
    int ret;
    int rule_id = 0;
    int matches = 0;
    int* matched_indexes;
    msgpack_object *key;
    msgpack_object *val;
    msgpack_object *s_key;
    msgpack_object *o_key;
    msgpack_object *o_val;
    struct mk_list *head;
    struct flb_mp_accessor_match *match;
    struct flb_mp_accessor_ra *mp_ra;
    struct flb_mp_map_header mh;
    msgpack_sbuffer mp_sbuf;
    msgpack_packer mp_pck;
    struct flb_mp_accessor_match *local_matches;
    size_t local_matches_size;

    if (map->via.map.size == 0) {
        return FLB_FALSE;
    }

    local_matches_size = mpa->matches_size;
    local_matches = flb_calloc(1, local_matches_size);
    if (!local_matches) {
        flb_errno();
        return -1;
    }

    mk_list_foreach(head, &mpa->ra_list) {
        mp_ra = mk_list_entry(head, struct flb_mp_accessor_ra, _head);

        if (mp_ra->is_active == FLB_FALSE) {
            rule_id++;
            continue;
        }

        /* Apply the record accessor rule against the map */
        ret = flb_ra_get_kv_pair(mp_ra->ra, *map, &s_key, &o_key, &o_val);
        if (ret == 0) {
            /* There is a match, register in the matches table */
            match = &local_matches[rule_id];
            match->matched = FLB_TRUE;
            match->start_key = s_key;        /* Initial key path that matched */
            match->key = o_key;              /* Final key that matched */
            match->val = o_val;              /* Final value */
            match->ra = mp_ra->ra;           /* Record accessor context */
            matches++;
        }
        rule_id++;
    }

    /* If no matches, no modifications were made */
    if (matches == 0) {
        flb_free(local_matches);
        return FLB_FALSE;
    }

    /* Some rules matched, compose a new outgoing buffer */
    msgpack_sbuffer_init(&mp_sbuf);
    msgpack_packer_init(&mp_pck, &mp_sbuf, msgpack_sbuffer_write);

    /* Initialize map */
    flb_mp_map_header_init(&mh, &mp_pck);

    /* Initialize array of matching indexes to properly handle sibling keys */
    matched_indexes = flb_malloc(sizeof(int) * matches);
    if (!matched_indexes) {
        flb_errno();
        flb_free(local_matches);
        msgpack_sbuffer_destroy(&mp_sbuf);
        return -1;
    }

    for (i = 0; i < map->via.map.size; i++) {
        key = &map->via.map.ptr[i].key;
        val = &map->via.map.ptr[i].val;

        /*
         * For every entry on the path, check if we should do a step-by-step
         * repackaging or just pack the whole object.
         *
         * Find all matching rules that match this '"'"'key'"'"'. Return the number of matches or 0
         * if no matches were found. Found matches are stored in the '"'"'matched_indexes'"'"' array.
         */
        
        int match_count = 0;
        int out_index = 0;
        int ra_count = mk_list_size(&mpa->ra_list);
        for (int j = 0; j < ra_count; j++) {
            match = &local_matches[j];
            if (match->matched == FLB_FALSE) {
                continue;
            }

            if (match->start_key == key) {
                match_count++;
                matched_indexes[out_index++] = j;
            }
        }

        if (match_count == 0) {
            /* No matches, it'"'"'s ok to pack the kv pair */
            flb_mp_map_header_append(&mh);
            msgpack_pack_object(&mp_pck, *key);
            msgpack_pack_object(&mp_pck, *val);
        }
        else {
            /* The key has a match. Now we do a step-by-step packaging */
            
            /* Since accessor_sub_pack still uses mpa->matches, we need to temporarily swap it 
               or rewrite accessor_sub_pack. Swapping is easier but needs a lock if multiple 
               threads use the same mpa. But the point is to make it thread safe.
            */
            /* Actually, accessor_sub_pack just needs the match information. Let'"'"'s rewrite it or 
               pass local_matches to it.
            */
            
            /* To keep it simple and correct, I will use a local copy of mpa->matches inside accessor_sub_pack as well. 
               This means accessor_sub_pack also needs to be updated.
            */
            
            /* I'"'"'ll stop here and rethink. The easiest way is to protect mpa->matches with a mutex inside flb_mp_accessor_keys_remove, 
               but wait, the caller might be using workers. If they all use the same mpa, they will contend. 
               The PR says Workers 2. Each worker has its own thread. 
            */
            /* If I use a lock, it will work but might be slow. But the current implementation is definitely not thread-safe. */
            
            /* Let'"'"'s see how mpa is created and stored. In Loki, it'"'"'s in ctx->remove_mpa. 
               ctx is the plugin instance. In Fluent Bit, plugin instances are shared among workers? 
               Yes, but some plugins have thread-local data. 
            */
            
            /* If I change accessor_sub_pack and accessor_key_find_matches to take the matches array as an argument, it becomes thread-safe. */
            
            flb_free(local_matches); /* dummy to satisfy the logic for now, I will redo the whole thing */
            flb_free(matched_indexes);
            msgpack_sbuffer_destroy(&mp_sbuf);
            return -1; 
        }
    }
    return -1;
}
    struct flb_mp_map_header mh;
    msgpack_sbuffer mp_sbuf;
    msgpack_packer mp_pck;

                                    struct flb_mp_accessor_match *local_matches,
                                    int* matched_indexes,
                                    int match_count,
                                    msgpack_packer *mp_pck,
                                    msgpack_object *key,
                                    msgpack_object *val)
{
    int i;
    int ret;
    msgpack_object *k;
    msgpack_object *v;
    struct flb_mp_map_header mh;
    struct flb_mp_accessor_match *match;

    for (i = 0; i < match_count; i++) {
        match = &local_matches[matched_indexes[i]];
        if (match->key == key || match->key == val) {
            return FLB_FALSE;
        }
    }

    if (key) {
        msgpack_pack_object(mp_pck, *key);
    }

    if (val->type == MSGPACK_OBJECT_MAP) {
        flb_mp_map_header_init(&mh, mp_pck);
        for (i = 0; i < val->via.map.size; i++) {
            k = &val->via.map.ptr[i].key;
            v = &val->via.map.ptr[i].val;

            ret = accessor_sub_pack(mpa, local_matches, matched_indexes, match_count, mp_pck, k, v);
            if (ret == FLB_TRUE) {
                flb_mp_map_header_append(&mh);
            }
        }
        flb_mp_map_header_end(&mh);
    }
    else if (val->type == MSGPACK_OBJECT_ARRAY) {
        flb_mp_array_header_init(&mh, mp_pck);
        for (i = 0; i < val->via.array.size; i++) {
            v = &val->via.array.ptr[i];
            ret = accessor_sub_pack(mpa, local_matches, matched_indexes, match_count, mp_pck, NULL, v);
            if (ret == FLB_TRUE) {
                flb_mp_array_header_append(&mh);
            }
        }
        flb_mp_array_header_end(&mh);
    }
    else {
        msgpack_pack_object(mp_pck, *val);
    }

    return FLB_TRUE;

/*
 * Remove keys or nested keys from a map. It compose the final result in a
 * new buffer. On error, it returns -1, if the map was modified it returns FLB_TRUE,
 * if no modification was required it returns FLB_FALSE.
 */
int flb_mp_accessor_keys_remove(struct flb_mp_accessor *mpa,
                                msgpack_object *map,
                                void **out_buf, size_t *out_size)
{
    int i;
    int ret;
    int rule_id = 0;
    int matches = 0;
    int* matched_indexes;
    msgpack_object *key;
    msgpack_object *val;
    msgpack_object *s_key;
    msgpack_object *o_key;
    msgpack_object *o_val;
    struct mk_list *head;
    struct flb_mp_accessor_match *match;
    struct flb_mp_accessor_ra *mp_ra;
    struct flb_mp_map_header mh;
    msgpack_sbuffer mp_sbuf;
    msgpack_packer mp_pck;
    struct flb_mp_accessor_match *local_matches;
    size_t local_matches_size;

    if (map->via.map.size == 0) {
        return FLB_FALSE;
    }

    local_matches_size = mpa->matches_size;
    local_matches = flb_calloc(1, local_matches_size);
    if (!local_matches) {
        flb_errno();
        return -1;
    }

    mk_list_foreach(head, &mpa->ra_list) {
        mp_ra = mk_list_entry(head, struct flb_mp_accessor_ra, _head);

        if (mp_ra->is_active == FLB_FALSE) {
            rule_id++;
            continue;
        }

        /* Apply the record accessor rule against the map */
        ret = flb_ra_get_kv_pair(mp_ra->ra, *map, &s_key, &o_key, &o_val);
        if (ret == 0) {
            /* There is a match, register in the local matches table */
            match = &local_matches[rule_id];
            match->matched = FLB_TRUE;
            match->start_key = s_key;        /* Initial key path that matched */
            match->key = o_key;              /* Final key that matched */
            match->val = o_val;              /* Final value */
            match->ra = mp_ra->ra;           /* Record accessor context */
            matches++;
        }
        rule_id++;
    }

    /* If no matches, no modifications were made */
    if (matches == 0) {
        flb_free(local_matches);
        return FLB_FALSE;
    }

    /* Some rules matched, compose a new outgoing buffer */
    msgpack_sbuffer_init(&mp_sbuf);
    msgpack_packer_init(&mp_pck, &mp_sbuf, msgpack_sbuffer_write);

    /* Initialize map */
    flb_mp_map_header_init(&mh, &mp_pck);

    /* Initialize array of matching indexes to properly handle sibling keys */
    matched_indexes = flb_malloc(sizeof(int) * matches);
    if (!matched_indexes) {
        flb_errno();
        flb_free(local_matches);
        msgpack_sbuffer_destroy(&mp_sbuf);
        return -1;
    }

    for (i = 0; i < map->via.map.size; i++) {
        key = &map->via.map.ptr[i].key;
        val = &map->via.map.ptr[i].val;

        /*
         * For every entry on the path, check if we should do a step-by-step
         * repackaging or just pack the whole object.
         *
         * Find all matching rules that match this '"'"'key'"'"'. Return the number of matches or 0
         * if no matches were found. Found matches are stored in the '"'"'matched_indexes'"'"' array.
         */
        int match_count = 0;
        int out_index = 0;
        int r_count = mk_list_size(&mpa->ra_list);
        for (int j = 0; j < r_count; j++) {
            match = &local_matches[j];
            if (match->matched == FLB_FALSE) {
                continue;
            }

            if (match->start_key == key) {
                match_count++;
                matched_indexes[out_index++] = j;
            }
        }

        if (match_count == 0) {
            /* No matches, it'"'"'s ok to pack the kv pair */
            flb_mp_map_header_append(&mh);
            msgpack_pack_object(&mp_pck, *key);
            msgpack_pack_object(&mp_pck, *val);
        }
        else {
            /* The key has a match. Now we do a step-by-step packaging */
            ret = accessor_sub_pack(mpa, local_matches, matched_indexes, match_count, &mp_pck, key, val);
            if (ret == FLB_TRUE) {
                flb_mp_map_header_append(&mh);
            }
        }
    }
    flb_mp_map_header_end(&mh);

    flb_free(matched_indexes);
    flb_free(local_matches);

    *out_buf = mp_sbuf.data;
    *out_size = mp_sbuf.size;

    return FLB_TRUE;
}

   815	
   816	void flb_mp_accessor_destroy(struct flb_mp_accessor *mpa)
   817	{
   818	    struct mk_list *tmp;
   819	    struct mk_list *head;
   820	    struct flb_mp_accessor_ra *mp_ra;
   821	
   822	    if (!mpa) {
   823	        return;
   824	    }
   825	
   826	    mk_list_foreach_safe(head, tmp, &mpa->ra_list) {
   827	        mp_ra = mk_list_entry(head, struct flb_mp_accessor_ra, _head);

        return FLB_FALSE;
    }

    /* Reset matches cache */
    memset(mpa->matches, '"'"'\0'"'"', mpa->matches_size);

    mk_list_foreach(head, &mpa->ra_list) {
        mp_ra = mk_list_entry(head, struct flb_mp_accessor_ra, _head);

        if (mp_ra->is_active == FLB_FALSE) {
            rule_id++;
            continue;
        }

        /* Apply the record accessor rule against the map */
        ret = flb_ra_get_kv_pair(mp_ra->ra, *map, &s_key, &o_key, &o_val);
        if (ret == 0) {
            /* There is a match, register in the matches table */
            match = &mpa->matches[rule_id];
            match->matched = FLB_TRUE;
            match->start_key = s_key;        /* Initial key path that matched */
            match->key = o_key;              /* Final key that matched */
            match->val = o_val;              /* Final value */
            match->ra = mp_ra->ra;           /* Record accessor context */
            matches++;
        }
        rule_id++;
    }

    /* If no matches, no modifications were made */
    if (matches == 0) {
        return FLB_FALSE;
    }

    /* Some rules matched, compose a new outgoing buffer */
    msgpack_sbuffer_init(&mp_sbuf);
    msgpack_packer_init(&mp_pck, &mp_sbuf, msgpack_sbuffer_write);

    /* Initialize map */
    flb_mp_map_header_init(&mh, &mp_pck);

    /* Initialize array of matching indexes to properly handle sibling keys */
    matched_indexes = flb_malloc(sizeof(int) * matches);
    if (!matched_indexes) {
        flb_errno();
        return -1;
    }

    for (i = 0; i < map->via.map.size; i++) {
        key = &map->via.map.ptr[i].key;
        val = &map->via.map.ptr[i].val;

        /*
         * For every entry on the path, check if we should do a step-by-step
         * repackaging or just pack the whole object.
         *
         * Find all matching rules that match this '"'"'key'"'"'. Return the number of matches or 0
         * if no matches were found. Found matches are stored in the '"'"'matched_indexes'"'"' array.
         */
        ret = accessor_key_find_matches(mpa, key, matched_indexes);
        if (ret == 0) {
            /* No matches, it'"'"'s ok to pack the kv pair */
            flb_mp_map_header_append(&mh);
            msgpack_pack_object(&mp_pck, *key);
            msgpack_pack_object(&mp_pck, *val);
        }
        else {
            /* The key has a match. Now we do a step-by-step packaging */

            ret = accessor_sub_pack(mpa, matched_indexes, ret, &mp_pck, key, val);
            if (ret == FLB_TRUE) {
                flb_mp_map_header_append(&mh);
            }
        }
    }
    flb_mp_map_header_end(&mh);

    flb_free(matched_indexes);

    *out_buf = mp_sbuf.data;
    *out_size = mp_sbuf.size;

    return FLB_TRUE;

            continue;
        }

        if (match->start_key == key) {
            match_count++;
            matched_indexes[out_index++] = i;
        }
    }

    return match_count;
}

   537	
   538	static inline int accessor_sub_pack(struct flb_mp_accessor *mpa,
   539	                                    struct flb_mp_accessor_match *local_matches,
   540	                                    int* matched_indexes,
   541	                                    int match_count,
   542	                                    msgpack_packer *mp_pck,
   543	                                    msgpack_object *key,
   544	                                    msgpack_object *val)
   545	{
   546	    int i;
   547	    int ret;
   548	    msgpack_object *k;
   549	    msgpack_object *v;
   550	    struct flb_mp_map_header mh;
   551	    struct flb_mp_accessor_match *match;
   552	
   553	    for (i = 0; i < match_count; i++) {
   554	        match = &local_matches[matched_indexes[i]];
   555	        if (match->key == key || match->key == val) {
   556	            return FLB_FALSE;
   557	        }
   558	    }
   559	
   560	    if (key) {
   561	        msgpack_pack_object(mp_pck, *key);
   562	    }
   563	
   564	    if (val->type == MSGPACK_OBJECT_MAP) {
   565	        flb_mp_map_header_init(&mh, mp_pck);
   566	        for (i = 0; i < val->via.map.size; i++) {
   567	            k = &val->via.map.ptr[i].key;
   568	            v = &val->via.map.ptr[i].val;
   569	
   570	            ret = accessor_sub_pack(mpa, local_matches, matched_indexes, match_count, mp_pck, k, v);
   571	            if (ret == FLB_TRUE) {
   572	                flb_mp_map_header_append(&mh);
   573	            }
   574	        }
   575	        flb_mp_map_header_end(&mh);
   576	    }
   577	    else if (val->type == MSGPACK_OBJECT_ARRAY) {
   578	        flb_mp_array_header_init(&mh, mp_pck);
   579	        for (i = 0; i < val->via.array.size; i++) {
   580	            v = &val->via.array.ptr[i];
   581	            ret = accessor_sub_pack(mpa, local_matches, matched_indexes, match_count, mp_pck, NULL, v);
   582	            if (ret == FLB_TRUE) {
   583	                flb_mp_array_header_append(&mh);
   584	            }
   585	        }
   586	        flb_mp_array_header_end(&mh);
   587	    }
   588	    else {
   589	        msgpack_pack_object(mp_pck, *val);
   590	    }
   591	
   592	    return FLB_TRUE;
   593	}
   594	
   595	
   596	/*
   597	 * Remove keys or nested keys from a map. It compose the final result in a
   598	 * new buffer. On error, it returns -1, if the map was modified it returns FLB_TRUE,
   599	 * if no modification was required it returns FLB_FALSE.
   600	 */
   601	int flb_mp_accessor_keys_remove(struct flb_mp_accessor *mpa,
   602	                                msgpack_object *map,
   603	                                void **out_buf, size_t *out_size)
   604	{
   605	    int i;
   606	    int ret;
   607	    int rule_id = 0;
   608	    int matches = 0;
   609	    int* matched_indexes;
   610	    msgpack_object *key;
   611	    msgpack_object *val;
   612	    msgpack_object *s_key;
   613	    msgpack_object *o_key;
   614	    msgpack_object *o_val;
   615	    struct mk_list *head;
   616	    struct flb_mp_accessor_match *match;
   617	    struct flb_mp_accessor_ra *mp_ra;
   618	    struct flb_mp_map_header mh;
   619	    msgpack_sbuffer mp_sbuf;
   620	    msgpack_packer mp_pck;
   621	    struct flb_mp_accessor_match *local_matches;
   622	    size_t local_matches_size;
   623	
   624	    if (map->via.map.size == 0) {
   625	        return FLB_FALSE;
   626	    }
   627	
   628	    local_matches_size = mpa->matches_size;
   629	    local_matches = flb_calloc(1, local_matches_size);
   630	    if (!local_matches) {
   631	        flb_errno();
   632	        return -1;
   633	    }
   634	
   635	    mk_list_foreach(head, &mpa->ra_list) {
   636	        mp_ra = mk_list_entry(head, struct flb_mp_accessor_ra, _head);
   637	
   638	        if (mp_ra->is_active == FLB_FALSE) {
   639	            rule_id++;
   640	            continue;
   641	        }
   642	
   643	        /* Apply the record accessor rule against the map */
   644	        ret = flb_ra_get_kv_pair(mp_ra->ra, *map, &s_key, &o_key, &o_val);
   645	        if (ret == 0) {
   646	            /* There is a match, register in the local matches table */
   647	            match = &local_matches[rule_id];
   648	            match->matched = FLB_TRUE;
   649	            match->start_key = s_key;        /* Initial key path that matched */
   650	            match->key = o_key;              /* Final key that matched */
   651	            match->val = o_val;              /* Final value */
   652	            match->ra = mp_ra->ra;           /* Record accessor context */
   653	            matches++;
   654	        }
   655	        rule_id++;
   656	    }
   657	
   658	    /* If no matches, no modifications were made */
   659	    if (matches == 0) {
   660	        flb_free(local_matches);
   661	        return FLB_FALSE;
   662	    }
   663	
   664	    /* Some rules matched, compose a new outgoing buffer */
   665	    msgpack_sbuffer_init(&mp_sbuf);
   666	    msgpack_packer_init(&mp_pck, &mp_sbuf, msgpack_sbuffer_write);
   667	
   668	    /* Initialize map */
   669	    flb_mp_map_header_init(&mh, &mp_pck);
   670	
   671	    /* Initialize array of matching indexes to properly handle sibling keys */
   672	    matched_indexes = flb_malloc(sizeof(int) * matches);
   673	    if (!matched_indexes) {
   674	        flb_errno();
   675	        flb_free(local_matches);
   676	        msgpack_sbuffer_destroy(&mp_sbuf);
   677	        return -1;
   678	    }
   679	
   680	    for (i = 0; i < map->via.map.size; i++) {
   681	        key = &map->via.map.ptr[i].key;
   682	        val = &map->via.map.ptr[i].val;
   683	
   684	        /*
   685	         * For every entry on the path, check if we should do a step-by-step
   686	         * repackaging or just pack the whole object.
   687	         *
   688	         * Find all matching rules that match this 'key'. Return the number of matches or 0
   689	         * if no matches were found. Found matches are stored in the 'matched_indexes' array.
   690	         */
   691	        ret = accessor_key_find_matches(mpa, local_matches, key, matched_indexes);
   692	        if (ret == 0) {
   693	            /* No matches, it's ok to pack the kv pair */
   694	            flb_mp_map_header_append(&mh);
   695	            msgpack_pack_object(&mp_pck, *key);
   696	            msgpack_pack_object(&mp_pck, *val);
   697	        }
   698	        else {
   699	            /* The key has a match. Now we do a step-by-step packaging */
   700	            ret = accessor_sub_pack(mpa, local_matches, matched_indexes, ret, &mp_pck, key, val);
   701	            if (ret == FLB_TRUE) {
   702	                flb_mp_map_header_append(&mh);
   703	            }
   704	        }
   705	    }
   706	    flb_mp_map_header_end(&mh);
   707	
   708	    flb_free(matched_indexes);
   709	    flb_free(local_matches);
   710	
   711	    *out_buf = mp_sbuf.data;
   712	    *out_size = mp_sbuf.size;
   713	
   714	    return FLB_TRUE;
   715	}
   716	
   717	void flb_mp_accessor_destroy(struct flb_mp_accessor *mpa)
   718	{
   719	    struct mk_list *tmp;
   720	    struct mk_list *head;
   721	    struct flb_mp_accessor_ra *mp_ra;
   722	
   723	    if (!mpa) {
   724	        return;
   725	    }
   726	
   727	    mk_list_foreach_safe(head, tmp, &mpa->ra_list) {
   728	        mp_ra = mk_list_entry(head, struct flb_mp_accessor_ra, _head);
   729	        mk_list_del(&mp_ra->_head);
   730	        flb_ra_destroy(mp_ra->ra);
